GRU_hydroelectricity_decisions = {
	GRU_Damn_the_danube_decision = {
		icon = generic_construction

		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = GRU_hydroelectric_power
			4 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
		}
		available = {
			has_completed_focus = GRU_hydroelectric_power
			4 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = GRU_HYDRO_BUILDING }
		}
		fire_only_once = yes
		cost = 20
		days_remove = 100

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 6
		}
		
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision GRU_Damn_the_danube_decision"
			set_country_flag = GRU_HYDRO_BUILDING
		}
		
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove GRU_Damn_the_danube_decision"
			clr_country_flag = GRU_HYDRO_BUILDING
			4 = {
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 2
					instant_build = yes
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = dam
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
					province = {
						id = 11651
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = {
					localization_key = building_state_modifier|dam
					INDENT = "    "
				}
			}
		}
	}

	GRU_DAF_Volkswagen_decision = {
		icon = GFX_Volkswagen

		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = GRU_DAF
		}
		available = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = GRU_KDF_ONGOING_PROJECT }
		}
		fire_only_once = yes
		cost = 120
		days_remove = 100

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 6
		}
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = GRU_KDF_ONGOING_PROJECT
		}
		remove_effect = {

			hidden_effect = {
				GRU= {	country_event = rotermorgenmisc.9 }
			}
		}
	}

				}
			}
		}
		targets = { AUS }
		target_root_trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = GRU_NMDVP_PAN_GERMANISM
		}

		target_trigger = {
			can_declare_war_on = FROM
			FROM = {
				OR = {
				tag = AUS
				}	
			}
		}

		fire_only_once = yes
		cost = 50
		days_remove = 30

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 150
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_war = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio < 0.8
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = {
					any_allied_country = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
						overlord = {
							strength_ratio = {
								tag = ROOT
								ratio > 0.7
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = {
					is_subject = yes
					overlord = {
						strength_ratio = {
							tag = ROOT
							ratio > 0.7
						}
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = imminent_war
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision GRU_pan_germanism_austria_decision target: [From.GetName]"
			set_country_flag = { flag = imminent_war days = 30 value = 1 }
			FROM = {
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = prepare_for_war
					id = ROOT
					value = 1000
				}
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove GRU_pan_germanism_austria_decision target: [From.GetName]"
			FROM = {
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = prepare_for_war
					id = ROOT
					value = -1000
				}
			}
			declare_war_on = {	type = annex_everything	target = AUS }
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = { is_core_of = AUS is_core_of = SLO is_core_of = FIU }
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
	}

	GRU_volksland_hypoborea = {

			icon = GFX_hypoboreaVK
			ai_will_do = {
				factor = 50
			}
			fire_only_once = yes
				
			available = {
				has_completed_focus = GRU_NMDVP_LEBENSRAUM
				has_completed_focus = GRU_NMDVP_SCANDINAVIA
				tag = GRU 
						OR = {
							GRU = {
								owns_state = 141
							}
							any_other_country = {
								is_subject_of = GRU
								owns_state = 141
						}
					}
				}
		
			visible = {
				has_completed_focus = GRU_NMDVP_LEBENSRAUM
				has_completed_focus = GRU_NMDVP_SCANDINAVIA
			}
		
			complete_effect = {
				create_HYP = yes
				hidden_effect = {
					HYP = {
						transfer_state = 141
						
						add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = infantry_equipment_1
						amount = 4000
						} 
						add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = support_equipment
						amount = 100
						}
						add_manpower = 40000
					}
				HYP = {	country_event = rotermorgenmisc.900 }
					if = {
						limit = {
							GRU = { has_country_flag = NMDVP_R_RULE }
						}
						HYP = {	
							set_popularities = {
								national_populist = 100
							}
							set_politics = {
								ruling_party = national_populist
								last_election = "1936.1.1"
								election_frequency = 48
								elections_allowed = no
							}
						}
					}
				}
				set_autonomy = { target = HYP autonomy_state = RM_Volksland }
				set_country_flag = HYP_established
				HYP = { set_country_flag = IS_HYP }
				HYP = { inherit_technology = GRU }
			}
	}

					tag = FROM

				}

					type = prepare_for_war
					id = ROOT
					value = 1000
				}
			}
		}

					type = prepare_for_war

					value = -1000

						}

							set_popularities = {

								elections_allowed = no

						}

				set_country_flag = VST_established
				VST = { set_country_flag = IS_VST }
				VST = { inherit_technology = GRU }
			}

						OR = {
							tag = ROOT
							gives_military_access_to = ROOT
							is_in_faction_with = ROOT
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
				has_socialist_government = no
				NOT = { tag = RUS }
				NOT = { tag = TRM }
				NOT = { original_tag = UKR }
				NOT = { tag = WHR }
				NOT = { tag = ALO }
				NOT = { tag = DKB }
				NOT = { tag = AUS }
			}
		}

		target_array = global.european_tags_array

			has_completed_focus = GRU_SMEPD_LIBERATE_NEIGHBOURS
		}

		target_trigger = {
			can_declare_war_on = FROM

				OR = {
					any_neighbor_country = {

							tag = ROOT

GRU_stahlpakt_alliance_decisions = {
	
	GRU_stahlpakt_invite_countries_decision = {
		icon = generic_political_actions

		available = {
			is_major = yes
			is_subject = no
			is_faction_leader = yes
			has_war = no
			NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Reinhard Heydrich" ruling_only = yes } }
		}
		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = GRU_NMDVP_allignment
			NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Reinhard Heydrich" ruling_only = yes } }
			FROM = {
				is_possible_target_for_stahlpakt_alliance = yes
				is_not_excluded_from_stahlpakt_alliance = no
			}
		}

		target_root_trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = GRU_NMDVP_allignment
		}

		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				is_possible_target_for_stahlpakt_alliance = yes
				is_not_excluded_from_stahlpakt_alliance = no
			}
		}

		fire_only_once = no
		cost = 100
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 6
		}
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision GRU_stahlpakt_invite_countries_decision target: [From.GetName]"
			FROM = {	country_event = rotermorgenmisc.801 }
		}
	}
}
